        }

        function loadOneTrustScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();

            if (!shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            preloadBannerSdk();

            ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES.forEach((library) => {
                loadScript(library.url, "text/javascript", library.options);
            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SungWon_Cho" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:SungWon Cho">SungWon Cho</a>;<br /><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Emi_Lo" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Emi Lo">Emi Lo</a> (young)</div>

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="dablink"><i>For the chapter of the same name, see <a href="/wiki/Chapter_809" title="Chapter 809">Chapter 809</a>.</i></span></dd></dl>
<p><b>Master Nekomamushi</b> is a feline <a href="/wiki/Mink_Tribe" title="Mink Tribe">mink</a> and the guardian of the Whale Forest on <a href="/wiki/Zou" title="Zou">Zou</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-c809a_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c809a-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> dubbed the "<b>Ruler of Night</b>"<sup id="cite_ref-c807_6-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c807-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> as he formerly <a href="/wiki/King_(Title)" title="King (Title)">ruled</a> over the <a href="/wiki/Mokomo_Dukedom" title="Mokomo Dukedom">Mokomo Dukedom</a> from 6:00 PM to 6:00 AM.<sup id="cite_ref-c809b_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c809b-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> He and <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a> serve as retainers for the <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Family" title="Kouzuki Family">Kouzuki Family</a> of <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-c819_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c819-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> as members of the <a href="/wiki/Nine_Red_Scabbards" title="Nine Red Scabbards">Nine Red Scabbards</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c939_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c939-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Alongside Inuarashi he was once a member of the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a> and <a href="/wiki/Roger_Pirates" title="Roger Pirates">Roger Pirates</a>, serving under <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c820_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c820-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Pedro" title="Pedro">Pedro</a> has claimed that he and Inuarashi must not be allowed to die because "the world is waiting for them".<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He is an ally of the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Island_Saga" title="Whole Cake Island Saga">Whole Cake Island Saga</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country_Saga" title="Wano Country Saga">Wano Country Saga</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Nekomamushi is a large, yellow feline mink with dark brown stripes, sharp teeth, claws, and a very thick striped tail. He has wild, bushy blonde hair resembling a lion's mane running around his neck and down his back, and there is a scar running from the left side of his forehead down to his cheek.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> His outfit consists of a large robe decorated with circles, a haramaki around his waist, sandals, a light-colored shirt, and pants. In addition, he frequently smokes a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kiseru" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Kiseru">kiseru</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> Like all the retainers of the <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Family" title="Kouzuki Family">Kouzuki Family</a>, Nekomamushi bears the family crest somewhere on his body.<sup id="cite_ref-c817a_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c817a-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>While being tortured by <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a>, he lost his left hand and part of his left forearm<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> due to several members of the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a> spearing them off.<sup id="cite_ref-c816a_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c816a-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> At some point before his arrival at <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>, Nekomamushi replaced his lost hand with a prosthetic double-barreled gun.
</p>

</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 162px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 162px; height: 162px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/Nekomamushi_Thousand_Storm.png/revision/latest?cb=20181026182852" class="image"><img alt="Nekomamushi Thousand Storm" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="120" height="140" data-image-name="Nekomamushi Thousand Storm.png" data-image-key="Nekomamushi_Thousand_Storm.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/Nekomamushi_Thousand_Storm.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/120?cb=20181026182852" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Nekomamushi in <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Thousand_Storm" title="One Piece Thousand Storm">One Piece Thousand Storm</a></i>.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 162px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 162px; height: 162px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/46/Log_Jack_Alt.png/revision/latest?cb=20190514130612" class="image"><img alt="Log Jack Alt" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="100" height="140" data-image-name="Log Jack Alt.png" data-image-key="Log_Jack_Alt.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/46/Log_Jack_Alt.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/100?cb=20190514130612" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Nekomamushi's attire from <a href="/wiki/Home_Video_Releases/Seasons_16-20" title="Home Video Releases/Seasons 16-20">One Piece Log Collection</a>.
</div></span></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D3&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Nekomamushi takes great pride in his status as one of the Mokomo Dukedom's rulers alongside <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a>, having proclaimed the country to be his when the night came during his first encounter with <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a>. Unlike his former friend Inuarashi, Nekomamushi is aggressive and merciless; Inuarashi has described him as an "obstinate and stubborn imbecile", comparing him to Jack himself, and he is completely willing to damage the historical Mokomo Dukedom while fighting, referring to doing so as a "minor detail".<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Nekomamushi can be stubborn even when not angry, as demonstrated when he kept ignoring <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Tony Tony Chopper</a>'s orders to recuperate in order to have fun. He does not like to be ordered around, having claimed that he went to bed of his own volition rather than on Chopper's orders while being treated by the doctor, and describes himself as a "freedom-loving man"; in spite of his bravado, however, he is afraid of needles.<sup id="cite_ref-c814a_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c814a-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite his stubborn, sometimes abrasive behavior, Nekomamushi genuinely cares for his friends and fellow minks; he took care of <a href="/wiki/Bepo" title="Bepo">Bepo</a> and the other <a href="/wiki/Heart_Pirates" title="Heart Pirates">Heart Pirates</a> when they arrived on Zou<sup id="cite_ref-c806_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c806-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> and did not expect them to help him defend the Mokomo Dukedom against the Beasts Pirates, though he was impressed when they decided to do so anyway.<sup id="cite_ref-c810a_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c810a-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> Additionally, while being tortured by Jack and his men, Nekomamushi convinced the Beasts Pirates to aim their spears at him instead of at his incapacitated fellow minks.<sup id="cite_ref-c816a_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c816a-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> He is also firmly loyal and possesses an incredibly strong will, having absolutely refused to reveal that Raizo was on Zou despite extensive torture at the hands of Jack, even when he lost his arm, and was fully willing to risk the kingdom's destruction in order to protect his friend.<sup id="cite_ref-c816b_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c816b-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> His loyalty to his allies means that he will treat anyone who tries to harm them viciously, having claimed he will devour any intruders he finds.<sup id="cite_ref-c809c_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c809c-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/af/Nekomamushi_Distracted_By_a_Ball.png/revision/latest?cb=20161121002221" class="image"><img alt="Nekomamushi Distracted By a Ball" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="136" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Nekomamushi Distracted By a Ball.png" data-image-key="Nekomamushi_Distracted_By_a_Ball.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/af/Nekomamushi_Distracted_By_a_Ball.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161121002221" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/af/Nekomamushi_Distracted_By_a_Ball.png/revision/latest?cb=20161121002221" class="image"><img alt="Nekomamushi Distracted By a Ball" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/af/Nekomamushi_Distracted_By_a_Ball.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161121002221" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="136" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Nekomamushi Distracted By a Ball.png" data-image-key="Nekomamushi_Distracted_By_a_Ball.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/af/Nekomamushi_Distracted_By_a_Ball.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161121002221" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Nekomamushi_Distracted_By_a_Ball.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Nekomamushi is instantly distracted by the sight of a bouncing ball.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Nekomamushi has many feline behaviors that can sometimes get the better of him; he likes to lick his paws,<sup id="cite_ref-c809c_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c809c-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> play with balls and cat toys,<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> and eat catnip.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Unlike most cats, however, he loves taking baths and eating <a href="/wiki/Foods#Lasagna" title="Foods">lasagna</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c814a_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c814a-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Like many others, Nekomamushi has his own <a href="/wiki/Laughter_Style" title="Laughter Style">unique laugh</a>: "Goronyanya".<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> "Nya" is the Japanese onomatopoeia for a cat's meow, and "goro" may come from "gorogoro", the Japanese onomatopoeia for purring.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D4&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Allies">Allies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D5&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b1/Inuarashi_and_Nekomamushi_Reconcile.png/revision/latest?cb=20201017212600" class="image"><img alt="Inuarashi and Nekomamushi Reconcile" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Inuarashi and Nekomamushi Reconcile.png" data-image-key="Inuarashi_and_Nekomamushi_Reconcile.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b1/Inuarashi_and_Nekomamushi_Reconcile.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201017212600" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b1/Inuarashi_and_Nekomamushi_Reconcile.png/revision/latest?cb=20201017212600" class="image"><img alt="Inuarashi and Nekomamushi Reconcile" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b1/Inuarashi_and_Nekomamushi_Reconcile.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201017212600" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Inuarashi and Nekomamushi Reconcile.png" data-image-key="Inuarashi_and_Nekomamushi_Reconcile.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b1/Inuarashi_and_Nekomamushi_Reconcile.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201017212600" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Inuarashi_and_Nekomamushi_Reconcile.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Nekomamushi and Inuarashi reconcile.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Nekomamushi and Inuarashi were once friends, but their friendship became strained after Oden's execution<sup id="cite_ref-c920_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c920-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> as the two minks blamed each other for Oden's death.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Because of this, they avoid meeting face-to-face.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Upon accidentally meeting, they exchanged hostile words and insults before preparing to enter a battle to the death despite their respective injuries.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite their present-day enmity, Inuarashi and Nekomamushi agreed to form a truce in order to avoid agitating Momonosuke<sup id="cite_ref-c817b_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c817b-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> and while reminiscing about their past adventures, they became very jolly and friendly with each other again.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pedro">Pedro</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As <a href="/wiki/Pedro" title="Pedro">Pedro</a> was a member of the <a href="/wiki/Guardians" title="Guardians">Guardians</a> that served under him, Nekomamushi was on very good terms with Pedro. Later when Pedro requested that he be allowed to join the Sanji Retrieval Team on their mission, against the requests of the other minks who also wished to join, Nekomamushi granted only Pedro's request, as Pedro is the only one who could keep <a href="/wiki/Pekoms" title="Pekoms">Pekoms</a> in line.<sup id="cite_ref-c822_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c822-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later in Wano Country, after meeting up with <a href="/wiki/Shishilian" title="Shishilian">Shishilian</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bariete" title="Bariete">Bariete</a>, Nekomamushi learned of Pedro's death and that the one responsible <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Charlotte Perospero</a> was nearby, which though he was happy that Pedro died for a noble cause Nekomamushi was determined to avenge Pedro's death.<sup id="cite_ref-c1012_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1012-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> After Nekomamushi knocked him out of the Skull Dome so they could have their battle elsewhere,<sup id="cite_ref-c1022_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1022-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> and transforming into his <a href="/wiki/Sulong" title="Sulong">Sulong</a>, Nekomamushi admitted if it had not been for Pedro's sacrifice then Luffy's mission to retrieve Sanji, and by extension the raid on <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>, would have ended in failure.<sup id="cite_ref-c1023_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1023-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> Though the odds in the battle turned against Nekomamushi when the storm clouds blocked out the full moon and cancelled out Nekomamushi's Sulong form resulting in terrible injuries, once the moon was visible again, a re-transformed Nekomamushi was able to defeat Perospero and avenge his comrade's death.<sup id="cite_ref-c1026_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1026-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kouzuki_Family">Kouzuki Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Due to Oden protecting him, <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kawamatsu" title="Kawamatsu">Kawamatsu</a> from discrimination during their youth, Nekomamushi is extremely loyal to the <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Family" title="Kouzuki Family">Kouzuki Family</a> of <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>, whom he serves as a retainer alongside Inuarashi.<sup id="cite_ref-c819_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c819-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> His loyalty to Oden and his family is so great that he risked sacrificing his kingdom and its inhabitants just to protect <a href="/wiki/Raizo" title="Raizo">Raizo</a>, another retainer of the clan,<sup id="cite_ref-c816b_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c816b-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> and later agreed to form a truce with his bitter rival Inuarashi in order to appease <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Momonosuke" title="Kouzuki Momonosuke">Kouzuki Momonosuke</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c817b_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c817b-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Nine_Red_Scabbards">Nine Red Scabbards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 300px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20230303041405" class="image"><img alt="Scabbards Charge Kaidou" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="300" height="169" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Scabbards Charge Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20230303041405" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20230303041405" class="image"><img alt="Scabbards Charge Kaidou" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20230303041405" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="300" height="169" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Scabbards Charge Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20230303041405" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Nekomamushi, alongside the other Red Scabbards (with Izou taking Kanjuro's place), charges into battle.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Aside from Inuarashi, Nekomamushi has an extremely strong and close friendship with fellow members of the Nine Red Scabbards, even after twenty years of separation. Nekomamushi risked his life and kingdom to protect Raizo from Jack, absolutely refusing to reveal Raizo's whereabouts even when brutally tortured to the point of losing an arm. When Raizo questioned about the fate of his fellow minks from Jack's brutality, Nekomamushi could only silently apologize.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Heart_Pirates">Heart Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Nekomamushi took the <a href="/wiki/Heart_Pirates" title="Heart Pirates">Heart Pirates</a> because <a href="/wiki/Bepo" title="Bepo">Bepo</a> is a native of Zou.<sup id="cite_ref-c806_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c806-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> He did not expect them to help him fight <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a>, but Bepo insisted on defending his home, which impressed Nekomamushi.<sup id="cite_ref-c810a_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c810a-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Straw_Hat_Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Like the rest of the Mink Tribe, Nekomamushi is very grateful to the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a>, particularly <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>, for saving them.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> When Sanji was forced to leave Zou with Bege for his impending marriage, Nekomamushi understood his crewmates' anguish and asked <a href="/wiki/Wanda" title="Wanda">Wanda</a> and <a href="/wiki/Carrot" title="Carrot">Carrot</a> to not tell anyone what happened, which prompted <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> to thank him for his understanding.<sup id="cite_ref-c814b_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c814b-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> However, he is not completely compliant with <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Tony Tony Chopper</a>'s orders for him to recuperate due to them restricting his freedom.<sup id="cite_ref-c814a_17-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c814a-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> Along with Inuarashi, Nekomamushi believes that Luffy will become the Pirate King, having willingly showed him the Road Poneglyph at Zou.
</p><p>Upon learning of <a href="/wiki/Nico_Robin" title="Nico Robin">Nico Robin</a>'s ability to read <a href="/wiki/Poneglyph" title="Poneglyph">Poneglyphs</a>, Nekomamushi feared for her safety, but Robin assured him that her crewmates would protect her.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> He was later amused that Luffy has Shanks’ <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat" title="Straw Hat">Straw Hat</a> and was shocked to learn that <a href="/wiki/Franky" title="Franky">Franky</a> was <a href="/wiki/Tom" title="Tom">Tom</a>'s apprentice and that <a href="/wiki/Brook" title="Brook">Brook</a> was the sole survivor of the <a href="/wiki/Rumbar_Pirates" title="Rumbar Pirates">Rumbar Pirates</a> that <a href="/wiki/Crocus" title="Crocus">Crocus</a> had searched for.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Jack">Jack</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>When night fell during the first day of the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>' battle with the minks, Nekomamushi was immediately informed of Jack's invasion and wasted no time in rushing to the scene before immediately attacking the pirate.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> After Jack incapacitated the minks with <a href="/wiki/Koro" title="Koro">poison gas</a> and tortured him for information regarding Raizo's whereabouts, Nekomamushi swore that he would never forget Jack's actions and that his curse would follow the pirate until he died.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> He and <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a> later fought against <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a> again at <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>, this time using their <a href="/wiki/Sulong" title="Sulong">Sulong</a> forms, and ultimately defeated him.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Though Jack did partially recover from his injures,<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Inuarashi was able to defeat him once more on his own.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Charlotte_Perospero">Charlotte Perospero</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Due to <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Charlotte Perospero</a>'s role in Pedro's death, Nekomamushi developed an intense hatred toward Perospero.<sup id="cite_ref-c1012_32-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1012-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> During the battle in Onigashima, Nekomamushi singles out Perospero, and the two fight outside the Skull Dome.<sup id="cite_ref-c1022_33-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1022-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> Transforming into his Sulong form by the full moon, Nekomamushi swears this will be the final moonlight Perospero would ever see.<sup id="cite_ref-c1023_34-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1023-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> When the clouds covered the moon, resulting in Nekomamushi's transformation becoming undone, Perospero badly injured the mink and boasted about his own good luck. However, the clouds parted shortly after, and Nekomamushi mocked Perospero's luck while pulling off a final Sulong attack, defeating Perospero and avenging Pedro.<sup id="cite_ref-c1026_35-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1026-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Others">Others</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pekoms">Pekoms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As with Bepo, Nekomamushi cares for <a href="/wiki/Pekoms" title="Pekoms">Pekoms</a> despite his status as a pirate; upon finding Pekoms badly injured after being shot multiple times, Nekomamushi confronted <a href="/wiki/Capone_Bege" title="Capone Bege">Capone Bege</a>, who was nearby, and demanded to know who he was and why Pekoms was injured despite his own injuries having not yet fully healed.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>As one of the former two rulers of the Mokomo Dukedom, Nekomamushi held a large amount of influence over the <a href="/wiki/Mink_Tribe" title="Mink Tribe">Mink Tribe</a>, with the highest authority during nighttime.<sup id="cite_ref-c809b_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c809b-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> As the Guardian of the Whale Forest and the commander of the <a href="/wiki/Guardians" title="Guardians">Guardians</a>, Nekomamushi had full control over the forest's inhabitants,<sup id="cite_ref-c806_18-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c806-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> before he stepped down from his position.
</p><p>Nekomamushi is equal in power to his daytime counterpart and friend <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a>, which caused all of their battles to end in stalemates.<sup id="cite_ref-c809a_7-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c809a-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Nekomamushi fought evenly against <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a>, an All-Star of the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a> with a bounty of <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>1,000,000,000, before the latter poisoned him with <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Koro" title="Koro">Koro</a> gas.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> Even while Nekomamushi was recovering from severe injuries, <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a> confidently left the protection of his comrades from the <a href="/wiki/Fire_Tank_Pirates" title="Fire Tank Pirates">Fire Tank Pirates</a> to him, while <a href="/wiki/Capone_Bege" title="Capone Bege">Capone Bege</a> felt wary of facing him and called him a monster.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> During the <a href="/wiki/Raid_on_Onigashima" title="Raid on Onigashima">raid on Onigashima</a>, his Sulong-enhanced attacks were capable of injuring the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Emperor</a> <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>, who had assumed his <a href="/wiki/Uo_Uo_no_Mi,_Model:_Seiryu" title="Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu">Beast Form</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As a former pirate, Nekomamushi is an able seaman with enough navigational skill to lead a crew formed from his Guardians through the New World.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> In the anime, Nekomamushi also knows how to make <a href="/wiki/Vivre_Card" title="Vivre Card">Vivre Cards</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Electro" title="Electro">Electro</a></i></dd></dl>
<p>Noted as one of the two strongest minks of the Mokomo Dukedom, Nekomamushi possesses immense physical strength, demonstrated when he lifted up Jack, in his <a href="/wiki/Zou_Zou_no_Mi,_Model:_Mammoth" title="Zou Zou no Mi, Model: Mammoth">Beast Form</a>, before slamming him into a building with enough force to destroy it.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> His claws are incredibly sharp and powerful, as he instantly beheaded <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Orochi" title="Kurozumi Orochi">Kurozumi Orochi</a> in his <a href="/wiki/Hebi_Hebi_no_Mi,_Model:_Yamata_no_Orochi" title="Hebi Hebi no Mi, Model: Yamata no Orochi">Beast Form</a><sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> and sent <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Charlotte Perospero</a> flying through a rock formation with a single swipe.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Despite his large size, Nekomamushi is also extremely fast and agile; he traveled from the Whale Forest to Kurau City in a matter of seconds and lept high into the air in the <a href="/wiki/Skull_Dome" title="Skull Dome">Skull Dome</a>. He has astounding levels of vitality as he fought against Jack and his replenishing forces for five days, taking 12-hour intervals to recover, and still managed to survive exposure to the Koro gas and an entire day of torture, which included the loss of his right arm.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> Even more notably, while all the other minks were immediately weakened and left unable to move by the <a href="/wiki/Koro" title="Koro">Koro</a> gas, Nekomamushi retained much of his strength and almost tore apart the chains that bound him to his crucifix, demonstrating an exceptional level of endurance.<sup id="cite_ref-c816a_16-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c816a-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> Like all minks, he can use <a href="/wiki/Electro" title="Electro">Electro</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c810b_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c810b-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>It is unknown how much the loss of his hand affects his overall combat abilities, but he managed to clash evenly with a one-legged <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> He was also able to disarm Kaidou of his kanabo and held his left arm to prevent him from retaliating against the ambush.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sulong_Form">Sulong Form</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Sulong" title="Sulong">Sulong</a></i></dd></dl>
<p>As a member of the <a href="/wiki/Mink_Tribe" title="Mink Tribe">Mink Tribe</a>, Nekomamushi can awaken the Sulong transformation when looking at the full moon. In this form, Nekomamushi's strength, speed, agility, Electro, and fighting abilities are magnified, allowing him to take out multiple members of the <a href="/wiki/Beast_Pirates" class="mw-redirect" title="Beast Pirates">Beast Pirates</a> and completely overwhelm Jack alongside Inuarashi and would have killed him if Kaidou had not intervened. A great testament to his power is that he defeated Charlotte Perospero, a pirate with a bounty of <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>700.000.000 and one of the strongest members of the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates" title="Big Mom Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</a>, with a single attack.<sup id="cite_ref-c1026_35-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1026-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Using this form is risky as it can cause severe exhaustion if used for too long. However, he can revert to his normal form by blocking his eyes from the moonlight.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Swordsmanship">Swordsmanship</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Oden_Two_Sword_Style" title="Oden Two Sword Style">Oden Two Sword Style</a></i></dd></dl>
<p>Nekomamushi has considerable skills in swordsmanship, able to fight on par with Inuarashi when they sparred during their youth.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> Like Inuarashi, his swordsmanship skill is great enough that he is capable of emulating Oden's signature Oden Two Sword Style, and even using a more personal version known as Oden One Sword Style.<sup id="cite_ref-c1026_35-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1026-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weapons">Weapons</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Nekomamushi wields a <a href="/wiki/Polearm#Partisan" title="Polearm">staff</a> resembling a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yari" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Yari">jumonji yari</a> with a fire-shaped blade on each end, which he can channel Electro through.<sup id="cite_ref-c810b_54-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c810b-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When he arrived at Wano, his lost left hand had been replaced with a double-barreled gun.<sup id="cite_ref-c984_60-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c984-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 172px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 172px; height: 142px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/45/Nekomamushi%27s_Partisan.png/revision/latest?cb=20161119231824" class="image"><img alt="Nekomamushi&#39;s Partisan" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="139" height="120" data-image-name="Nekomamushi&#39;s Partisan.png" data-image-key="Nekomamushi%27s_Partisan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/45/Nekomamushi%27s_Partisan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/139?cb=20161119231824" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Nekomamushi's staff.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 172px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 172px; height: 142px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b5/Nekomamushi%27s_Gun_Hand.png/revision/latest?cb=20230115170243" class="image"><img alt="Nekomamushi&#39;s Gun Hand" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="84" data-image-name="Nekomamushi&#39;s Gun Hand.png" data-image-key="Nekomamushi%27s_Gun_Hand.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b5/Nekomamushi%27s_Gun_Hand.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20230115170243" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Nekomamushi's prosthetic double-barreled gun.
</div></span></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Haki">Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>Nekomamushi possesses the ability to use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament</a> and <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past">Past</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_Years">Early Years</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In the distant past, Nekomamushi and <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a> were best friends.<sup id="cite_ref-c809a_7-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c809a-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> When they were children, they were told of the pact the <a href="/wiki/Mink_Tribe" title="Mink Tribe">Mink Tribe</a> made with the <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Family" title="Kouzuki Family">Kouzuki Family</a>. Curious, they left <a href="/wiki/Zou" title="Zou">Zou</a> and journeyed to <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>, but got shipwrecked. They were discovered at Kuri Beach by <a href="/wiki/Kawamatsu" title="Kawamatsu">Kawamatsu</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> Afterwards, the three were caught and persecuted by some humans until <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a> came and rescued them. They then followed Oden back to <a href="/wiki/Kuri" title="Kuri">Kuri</a> and became his retainers.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Oden%27s_Retainers_Caught_by_Yasuie.png/revision/latest?cb=20210214035702" class="image"><img alt="Oden&#39;s Retainers Caught by Yasuie" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Oden&#39;s Retainers Caught by Yasuie.png" data-image-key="Oden%27s_Retainers_Caught_by_Yasuie.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Oden%27s_Retainers_Caught_by_Yasuie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210214035702" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Oden%27s_Retainers_Caught_by_Yasuie.png/revision/latest?cb=20210214035702" class="image"><img alt="Oden&#39;s Retainers Caught by Yasuie" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Oden%27s_Retainers_Caught_by_Yasuie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210214035702" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Oden&#39;s Retainers Caught by Yasuie.png" data-image-key="Oden%27s_Retainers_Caught_by_Yasuie.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Oden%27s_Retainers_Caught_by_Yasuie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210214035702" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Oden%27s_Retainers_Caught_by_Yasuie.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A young Nekomamushi along with his fellow Scabbards after they were caught stealing by Yasuie.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When they were running low on funds, the retainers attempted to steal money from <a href="/wiki/Shimotsuki_Yasuie" title="Shimotsuki Yasuie">Shimotsuki Yasuie</a>, but they were caught. Instead of punishing them, Yasuie allowed them to take the money and encouraged them to use it to become better people for the sake of Oden and Wano.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> Following Yasuie's advice, they educated themselves and trained to become dignified warriors. 30 years ago, they visited the <a href="/wiki/Flower_Capital" title="Flower Capital">Flower Capital</a> with Oden.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After meeting the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a>, Oden and his retainers had a feast with them. Nekomamushi and Inuarashi also learned from <a href="/wiki/Marco" title="Marco">Marco</a> on how vast the world is. Two weeks later, the two minks stowed away on <a href="/wiki/Moby_Dick" title="Moby Dick">Whitebeard's ship</a> before they left Wano, knowing that Oden would not stop wanting to get on their ship. They revealed themselves after <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a> accepted Oden into the crew three days later. Afterwards, they traveled the seas together with the crew.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Two years later after the birth of <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Momonosuke" title="Kouzuki Momonosuke">Kouzuki Momonosuke</a> and Oden got a <a href="/wiki/Bounties" title="Bounties">bounty</a>, Nekomamushi noticed that the <a href="/wiki/Newspaper" title="Newspaper">newspaper</a> hardly had any news about Wano Country.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Around 26 years ago, sometime after the birth of <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Hiyori" title="Kouzuki Hiyori">Kouzuki Hiyori</a>, the Whitebeard Pirates clashed with the <a href="/wiki/Roger_Pirates" title="Roger Pirates">Roger Pirates</a> on an island for three days and three nights before the skirmish turned into a gift exchange and Oden decided to join <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a> to assist him with his final journey. Nekomamushi and Inuarashi boarded the <a href="/wiki/Oro_Jackson" title="Oro Jackson">Oro Jackson</a> as stowaways.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The two minks and Oden then sailed with Roger, and they visited <a href="/wiki/Skypiea" title="Skypiea">Skypiea</a> at one point. When the crew sailed to <a href="/wiki/Water_7" title="Water 7">Water 7</a>, the minks revealed to Roger about the Road <a href="/wiki/Poneglyph" title="Poneglyph">Poneglyph</a> at Zou. The Roger Pirates' voyage later took them to <a href="/wiki/Tequila_Wolf" title="Tequila Wolf">Tequila Wolf</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Fish-Man_Island" title="Fish-Man Island">Fish-Man Island</a>. Sometime after the visit to Fish-Man Island, <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Toki" title="Kouzuki Toki">Toki</a> became ill and the crew stopped by at Wano. The two minks chose to stay at Wano with Toki and her children, so they never went with Oden to <a href="/wiki/Laugh_Tale" title="Laugh Tale">Laugh Tale</a>. Before parting ways with Roger, Nekomamushi and Inuarashi gave him a letter of introduction for the Mink Tribe.<sup id="cite_ref-c820_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c820-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Nekomamushi and Inuarashi told <a href="/wiki/Kikunojo" title="Kikunojo">Kikunojo</a> about <a href="/wiki/Izou" title="Izou">Izou</a>'s stay with the Whitebeard Pirates. Around six months before Oden finished his voyage, Nekomamushi and his fellow retainers were furious at <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Orochi" title="Kurozumi Orochi">Kurozumi Orochi</a> for abusing his position as shogun. While Inuarashi and Kawamatsu stayed behind at Oden Castle, the other retainers marched to the Flower Capital to confront Orochi only to discover that a group of <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a> were in Kuri threatening Oden's family. When Oden returned to Wano after finishing his journey, the retainers (except <a href="/wiki/Denjiro" title="Denjiro">Denjiro</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ashura_Doji" title="Ashura Doji">Ashura Doji</a>, who were elsewhere at the time) welcomed him back and told him about Wano's situation. Oden then ordered his retainers to protect his family and Kuri before charging to the capital by himself.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Oden failed to kill Orochi, the retainers remained loyal to him for the next five years despite Oden acting like a fool and losing the respect of most of Wano's people. 20 years ago, Oden finally had enough and decided to take down <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>. The retainers eagerly followed him and marched with him to Onigashima.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> On the way to Onigashima, the group was confronted by Kaidou and his crew in the <a href="/wiki/Udon" title="Udon">Udon</a> region. In the ensuing battle, the samurai were joined by <a href="/wiki/Shinobu" title="Shinobu">Shinobu</a>. Unfortunately, the samurai were overwhelmed in the end. Oden and the Scabbards were then imprisoned in the Flower Capital and sentenced to be boiled alive in three days.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>All ten prisoners were later brought to the execution site, at which point Oden made a deal with Kaidou. After Oden stepped into the pot of boiling oil, the retainers were about to join him, but Oden grabbed a plank and ordered them to stand on it as he held them over the pot.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> As Oden endured <a href="/wiki/Legendary_Hour" title="Legendary Hour">the hour</a>, he explained to his retainers the reason Wano Country was isolated and requested them to open Wano's borders for him. Oden successfully survived the hour, but Orochi summoned a firing squad to execute Oden and his retainers. Oden once again told his retainers to open Wano's borders before throwing them far away from the pot. The Scabbards fled with tears as Oden met his demise.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Oden's death, Nekomamushi and Inuarashi began quarreling with each other on the way to Oden Castle. The two minks were captured by Orochi's forces, and they were left behind by the other retainers.<sup id="cite_ref-c920_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c920-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> They eventually managed to escape and returned to Zou barely alive, but they continued their feud to the point that they began fighting whenever they were together,<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> so they decided that Inuarashi would rule Zou during the day and Nekomamushi would rule during the night.<sup id="cite_ref-c809b_12-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c809b-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="During_the_Timeskip">During the Timeskip</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>When <a href="/wiki/Bepo" title="Bepo">Bepo</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Heart_Pirates" title="Heart Pirates">Heart Pirates</a> arrived, Nekomamushi took them under his care because, despite his status as a <a href="/wiki/Pirate" title="Pirate">pirate</a>, Bepo was a native of the island.<sup id="cite_ref-c806_18-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c806-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/35/Nekomamushi_Flips_Jack.png/revision/latest?cb=20161119231621" class="image"><img alt="Nekomamushi Flips Jack" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Nekomamushi Flips Jack.png" data-image-key="Nekomamushi_Flips_Jack.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/35/Nekomamushi_Flips_Jack.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161119231621" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/35/Nekomamushi_Flips_Jack.png/revision/latest?cb=20161119231621" class="image"><img alt="Nekomamushi Flips Jack" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/35/Nekomamushi_Flips_Jack.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161119231621" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Nekomamushi Flips Jack.png" data-image-key="Nekomamushi_Flips_Jack.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/35/Nekomamushi_Flips_Jack.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161119231621" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Nekomamushi_Flips_Jack.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Nekomamushi attacks Jack.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a> and the Beasts Pirates' invasion of Zou, Nekomamushi took over the battle as night fell. He quickly emerged from his domain and engaged in battle with Jack by flipping the latter over.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> Nekomamushi then prepared to continue fighting Jack, and was pleased to see the Heart Pirates assisting the <a href="/wiki/Guardians" title="Guardians">Guardians</a> in the battle.
