He fought Jack for five straight nights, switching out with Inuarashi once 6:00 AM arrived. Finally, Jack lost patience and used the <a href="/wiki/Koro" title="Koro">Koro</a> gas on the minks. He then crucified Nekomamushi, Inuarashi, and other strong minks and tortured them for <a href="/wiki/Raizo" title="Raizo">Raizo</a>'s whereabouts. However, the minks unwaveringly refused to give the ninja's location, and Nekomamushi nearly broke free from his chains, leading Jack and his men to sever his arm.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dressrosa_Saga">Dressrosa Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Dressrosa_Arc">Dressrosa Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>One day later, Jack left Zou when he learned of <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Doflamingo</a>'s defeat and capture, leaving some subordinates in the territory. Then the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> led by <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a> arrived.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> Once they chased away the remaining pirates and neutralised Koro, the pirates tended to Nekomamushi and the wounded minks.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Whole_Cake_Island_Saga">Whole Cake Island Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zou_Arc">Zou Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4e/Nekomamushi_Confronts_Bege.png/revision/latest?cb=20231128000037" class="image"><img alt="Nekomamushi Confronts Bege" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="166" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Nekomamushi Confronts Bege.png" data-image-key="Nekomamushi_Confronts_Bege.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4e/Nekomamushi_Confronts_Bege.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231128000037" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4e/Nekomamushi_Confronts_Bege.png/revision/latest?cb=20231128000037" class="image"><img alt="Nekomamushi Confronts Bege" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4e/Nekomamushi_Confronts_Bege.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231128000037" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="166" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Nekomamushi Confronts Bege.png" data-image-key="Nekomamushi_Confronts_Bege.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4e/Nekomamushi_Confronts_Bege.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231128000037" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Nekomamushi_Confronts_Bege.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Nekomamushi confronts Bege after discovering an injured Pekoms.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Several days later, while <a href="/wiki/Capone_Bege" title="Capone Bege">Capone Bege</a> was dealing with Sanji <a href="/wiki/Shiro_Shiro_no_Mi" title="Shiro Shiro no Mi">inside his body</a>, Nekomamushi confronted Bege after finding an injured <a href="/wiki/Pekoms" title="Pekoms">Pekoms</a>, which prompted Sanji to throw his crewmates out of Bege's body. Not wanting to fight Nekomamushi despite his visible injuries, Bege fled with Sanji and <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> Realizing that the remaining Straw Hats wanted the minks present to forget about what just happened, Nekomamushi told <a href="/wiki/Wanda" title="Wanda">Wanda</a> and <a href="/wiki/Carrot" title="Carrot">Carrot</a> to keep quiet about the incident and decided to look after Pekoms.<sup id="cite_ref-c814b_37-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c814b-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> and his group came to Zou, <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Tony Tony Chopper</a> went to check up on Nekomamushi after visiting Inuarashi.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> Nekomamushi was disobeying Chopper's orders by eating lasagna and taking a bath and was quickly forced back into bed as Chopper gave him more medical treatments.<sup id="cite_ref-c814a_17-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c814a-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> Shortly afterward, Nekomamushi left his bed and followed the other Straw Hats in order to meet Luffy and <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a>. After <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Trafalgar Law</a> warned Luffy about the threat of <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a> and the danger that the country would be in if they stayed on Zou, Nekomamushi decided to party with the members of the alliance and the other minks.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Raizo_Is_Safe.png/revision/latest?cb=20161204162210" class="image"><img alt="Raizo Is Safe" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Raizo Is Safe.png" data-image-key="Raizo_Is_Safe.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Raizo_Is_Safe.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161204162210" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Raizo_Is_Safe.png/revision/latest?cb=20161204162210" class="image"><img alt="Raizo Is Safe" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Raizo_Is_Safe.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161204162210" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Raizo Is Safe.png" data-image-key="Raizo_Is_Safe.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Raizo_Is_Safe.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161204162210" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Raizo_Is_Safe.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Nekomamushi and Inuarashi reveal that Raizo is safe.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The next morning, Nekomamushi was alerted by <a href="/wiki/Bariete" title="Bariete">Bariete</a> ringing the bells to announce the arrival of the <a href="/wiki/Samurai" title="Samurai">samurai</a> <a href="/wiki/Kin%27emon" title="Kin&#39;emon">Kin'emon</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Kanjuro" title="Kurozumi Kanjuro">Kanjuro</a>. Nekomamushi led the Guardians to Kurau City in search of the samurai but encountered Inuarashi. The two quickly began arguing and briefly clashed before Kin'emon interrupted them, revealing his identity and asking about Raizo. Nekomamushi and the minks then revealed that Raizo was on Zou, and they had kept him safe all this time.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>While conversing with Kin'emon, Nekomamushi and Inuarashi began arguing again, prompting <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Momonosuke" title="Kouzuki Momonosuke">Kouzuki Momonosuke</a> to reprimand them for doing so because it would make <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">his father</a> sad to see them behaving like this. Not wanting to disappoint their lord, Nekomamushi and Inuarashi apologized and called a truce, to the delight of their fellow minks. Shortly afterward, Inuarashi and Nekomamushi escorted the samurai and the Straw Hats to a secret area in the Whale Forest where Raizo was hidden.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After <a href="/wiki/Nico_Robin" title="Nico Robin">Nico Robin</a> deciphered the <a href="/wiki/Poneglyph" title="Poneglyph">Road Poneglyph</a> hidden within the Whale Tree, Nekomamushi revealed the purpose of the Road Poneglyphs and the locations of two others. He, Inuarashi, and the samurai then revealed that the <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Family" title="Kouzuki Family">Kouzuki Family</a> invented the poneglyphs, but their ability to make them was lost after Oden was killed by Kaidou and Orochi.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After speaking more about Oden, Nekomamushi and Inuarashi offered the minks' help in fighting against Kaidou, and after Momonosuke petitioned Luffy for his help, the minks formed an alliance with the Kouzuki Family, Straw Hat Pirates, and Heart Pirates known as the <a href="/wiki/Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai_Alliance" title="Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance">Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As the group left the secret room, Nekomamushi realized that he recognized Luffy's straw hat, which prompted Inuarashi to reveal that he and Nekomamushi once traveled with Oden aboard the ships of both Whitebeard and Roger, though they never went to Laugh Tale. As he reminisced about his days of adventure, Nekomamushi happily danced with Inuarashi while he did the same. Promising to one day detail all of Oden's adventures, Nekomamushi continued descending the Whale Tree while revealing that they intended to find and recruit <a href="/wiki/Marco" title="Marco">Marco</a>, whom he noted had vanished after clashing with <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Marshall D. Teach</a> a year ago during the <a href="/wiki/Payback_War" title="Payback War">Payback War</a>, though he had an idea of where Marco might be. Suddenly, Zou began shaking violently, causing a shocked Nekomamushi to realize that <a href="/wiki/Zunesha" title="Zunesha">Zunesha</a> was crying out before wondering to know what was going on.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> Jack's threat was ended when Momonosuke ordered Zunesha to destroy his fleet, but Nekomamushi was concerned about how Jack found Zou twice.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later on, <a href="/wiki/Pedro" title="Pedro">Pedro</a> and several other minks volunteered to join the Sanji Retrieval Team, but Nekomamushi decided to allow only Pedro to go because he could keep Pekoms in line. Soon afterward, as the Sanji Retrieval Team departed from Zou, Nekomamushi and the others were shocked when Luffy jumped off Zunesha with his party.<sup id="cite_ref-c822_31-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c822-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Saga">Wano Country Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Arc">Wano Country Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Nekomamushi and the Guardians located Marco at Whitebeard's home village, <a href="/wiki/Sphinx_(Location)" title="Sphinx (Location)">Sphinx</a>. As Nekomamushi spoke to Marco, the latter talked about Whitebeard's history with the village. Marco also heard about Edward Weevil attacking those connected to Whitebeard in search of a fortune that does not exist. After explaining that he could not leave because of the possibility that <a href="/wiki/Edward_Weevil" title="Edward Weevil">Edward Weevil</a> would attack the village as well, Marco asked Nekomamushi to pass on a message to Luffy,<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> which said that he would arrive at Wano at the last minute.
</p><p>However, Marco arrived at Wano along with Nekomamushi and <a href="/wiki/Izou" title="Izou">Izou</a>, making Marco's message unnecessary.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> After Nekomamushi's ship climbed the waterfall, Nekomamushi contacted his fellow Scabbards in the <a href="/wiki/Polar_Tang" title="Polar Tang">Polar Tang</a> and informed them that he would meet them at <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> Marco then dropped off Nekomamushi and Izou at Onigashima's back entrance, where they joined up with Law and the Scabbards with him.<sup id="cite_ref-c984_60-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c984-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Marco left to check on a shadow he saw at sea, the group was confronted by Kanjuro and an army of Beasts Pirates. While <a href="/wiki/Kikunojo" title="Kikunojo">Kikunojo</a> clashed against Kanjuro, the rest fought the other enemies.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> Kanjuro and the Beasts Pirates with him were defeated, and Nekomamushi's group were soon rejoined by Kin'emon and Denjiro. They then entered <a href="/wiki/Skull_Dome" title="Skull Dome">Kaidou's castle</a>, fought their way to the Live Stage, and launched an all-out attack on Kaidou.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> While falling to the lower floor, the Scabbards managed to inflict wounds on Kaidou. As the alliance revealed themselves and attacked the Beasts Pirates, Kaidou transformed into <a href="/wiki/Uo_Uo_no_Mi,_Model:_Seiryu" title="Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu">his Beast Form</a> and flew to the roof of the Skull Dome, with the Scabbards grabbing onto him. On the roof, the Scabbards prepared to fight Kaidou with the Mink Tribe's help.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> When Jack arrived to the roof with a platoon, Nekomamushi and Inuarashi's subjects urged their two leaders to focus on Kaidou.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> As Jack fought back against the minks, Nekomamushi and Inuarashi transformed into their <a href="/wiki/Sulong" title="Sulong">Sulong</a> forms and charged at Jack.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The two were able to badly wound Jack, to the point where Kaidou had to step in and call him off to rest. With Jack and his forces out of the way, the Scabbards and Izou resume their confrontation with Kaidou.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> Kaidou roared lightning at them, but they dodged around it and each struck him in turn.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> After suffering several injuries, Kaidou then retaliated with a roar that created wind scythes aimed at the Scabbards.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Continuing the battle in Human Form, Kaidou began overwhelming the Scabbards<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> and later incapacitated them. <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>, <a href="/wiki/Eustass_Kid" title="Eustass Kid">Eustass Kid</a>, <a href="/wiki/Killer" title="Killer">Killer</a>, Zoro, Luffy, and Law later arrived at the roof. Upon Luffy's request, Law <a href="/wiki/Ope_Ope_no_Mi" title="Ope Ope no Mi">teleported</a> the Scabbards to a safe place.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> They were placed in the treasure room on the second floor, where a mysterious person was tending to them.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup> The Scabbards later recovered and regained consciousness, but the mysterious figure already had left. Before they left the treasure room, they saw who appeared to be Oden.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> Many of the Scabbards believed it was him; however, "Oden" was quickly exposed to be a drawing made by Kanjuro, who was still alive and heading for Momonosuke. The Oden drawing then lit a large quantity of <a href="/wiki/Explosive#Dynamite" title="Explosive">dynamite</a> under its garment, but Ashura Doji tackled it out of the room before it exploded, sacrificing himself to save his comrades.
</p><p>The Scabbards immediately headed out to find Kanjuro but, but were then confronted by Beasts Pirates All-Star <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a>; Inuarashi stayed behind to battle him.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> As they raced through the fortress, they encountered Orochi and <a href="/wiki/Fukurokuju" title="Fukurokuju">Fukurokuju</a>. Orochi transformed into his <a href="/wiki/Hebi_Hebi_no_Mi,_Model:_Yamata_no_Orochi" title="Hebi Hebi no Mi, Model: Yamata no Orochi">Beast Form</a> to take on the Scabbards, but they responded by swiftly decapitating his multiple heads at once. They continued on, with Raizo staying behind to fight Fukurokuju.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e9/Nekomamushi_Defeats_Perospero.png/revision/latest?cb=20230212023140" class="image"><img alt="Nekomamushi Defeats Perospero" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Nekomamushi Defeats Perospero.png" data-image-key="Nekomamushi_Defeats_Perospero.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e9/Nekomamushi_Defeats_Perospero.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230212023140" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e9/Nekomamushi_Defeats_Perospero.png/revision/latest?cb=20230212023140" class="image"><img alt="Nekomamushi Defeats Perospero" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e9/Nekomamushi_Defeats_Perospero.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230212023140" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Nekomamushi Defeats Perospero.png" data-image-key="Nekomamushi_Defeats_Perospero.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e9/Nekomamushi_Defeats_Perospero.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230212023140" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Nekomamushi_Defeats_Perospero.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Nekomamushi defeats Perospero.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As the group moved through the castle, they encountered <a href="/wiki/Shishilian" title="Shishilian">Shishilian</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bariete" title="Bariete">Bariete</a>, who informed Nekomamushi that Carrot and Wanda were engaged in combat with <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Charlotte Perospero</a>, the man responsible for Pedro's death. Nekomamushi resolved to take revenge for Pedro and leapt far ahead of the other Scabbards.<sup id="cite_ref-c1012_32-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1012-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> Later, when Perospero attempted to attack Sanji during his fight with Queen, and after having his identity confirmed by Shishilian, Nekomamushi knocked Perospero outside of the Skull Dome to avenge Pedro's death, and immediately chased after him.<sup id="cite_ref-c1022_33-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1022-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> Outside, upon using the moonlight to transform once again into his Sulong form, Nekomamushi swears this will be the last moonlight that Perospero will ever see.<sup id="cite_ref-c1023_34-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1023-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> Though Nekomamushi was eventually placed at a huge disadvantage and was badly injured due to the the storm clouds caused by Kaidou and Momonosuke's dragon forms blocking off the full moon causing him to revert back, once the clouds parted due to the clashing of advanced grade <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>, Nekomamushi was able to regain his Sulong form and swiftly defeated Perospero with <i>Oden One Sword Style: Neko Niko Ban</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1026_35-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1026-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Back in the castle, they joined the resurging battle against the Beasts Pirates, who once again started to fight the Alliance's forces.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Luffy defeated Kaidou and Momonosuke safely landed the island, Nekomamushi announced to the forces that the Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance was victorious. When a volcano erupted where Onigashima once sat, Momonosuke flew with his sister and retainers into the Flower Capital in order to calm the panicking citizens. As the citizens marveled at the return of the Nine Red Scabbards, Denjiro then announced Momonosuke as the new Shogun of Wano Country. After broadcasting a speech to the whole country, Momonosuke, along with his retainers, entered the shogun's castle.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7a/Aramaki_vs_the_Scabbards.png/revision/latest?cb=20231029020649" class="image"><img alt="Aramaki vs the Scabbards" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Aramaki vs the Scabbards.png" data-image-key="Aramaki_vs_the_Scabbards.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7a/Aramaki_vs_the_Scabbards.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231029020649" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7a/Aramaki_vs_the_Scabbards.png/revision/latest?cb=20231029020649" class="image"><img alt="Aramaki vs the Scabbards" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7a/Aramaki_vs_the_Scabbards.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231029020649" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Aramaki vs the Scabbards.png" data-image-key="Aramaki_vs_the_Scabbards.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7a/Aramaki_vs_the_Scabbards.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231029020649" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Aramaki_vs_the_Scabbards.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The samurai ready to protect Luffy from Ryokugyu.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>A week later, after Luffy and Zoro finally awoke, Nekomamushi joined the Straw Hats in their feasting and bath.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> They later enjoyed the ongoing festivities of the Flower Capital.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> When the Kouzuki Retainers noticed <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Aramaki" title="Aramaki">Ryokugyu</a>'s approach, several of them, including Nekomamushi, went out to stop him from entering the Flower Capital. Using <a href="/wiki/Mori_Mori_no_Mi" title="Mori Mori no Mi">his Devil Fruit powers</a>, Ryokugyu attacked the samurai and announced his intent to go after Luffy. They were joined by Yamato and Momonosuke, and the retainers became distressed as Ryokugyu restrained Momonosuke.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup> However, the battle was then ended by Shanks outside of Wano, although unknown to anyone but Ryokugyu.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Momonosuke_as_the_Shogun.png/revision/latest?cb=20231126020849" class="image"><img alt="Momonosuke as the Shogun" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Momonosuke as the Shogun.png" data-image-key="Momonosuke_as_the_Shogun.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Momonosuke_as_the_Shogun.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231126020849" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Momonosuke_as_the_Shogun.png/revision/latest?cb=20231126020849" class="image"><img alt="Momonosuke as the Shogun" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Momonosuke_as_the_Shogun.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231126020849" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Momonosuke as the Shogun.png" data-image-key="Momonosuke_as_the_Shogun.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Momonosuke_as_the_Shogun.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231126020849" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Momonosuke_as_the_Shogun.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The samurai with their new Shogun ready to rebuild Wano.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Nekomamushi alongside the rest of the group returned to the Flower Capital. Inside the Shogun Castle, he was present when Kin'emon explained why he was not with them during the fight and though Kin'emon apologized for his absence, Nekomamushi brushed that off and instead asked Kin'emon to give them an update on Tsuru's status. After Kin'emon gave them an update, Inuarashi summoned Carrot to him and Nekomamushi. As Carrot stood before them, Inuarashi explained that they would name Carrot as the next leader of the Zou Kingdom, much to the latter's shock and surprise, as they explained their motives to stay behind in Wano to protect Momonosuke. When Carrot was doubting her strength and leadership qualities, they explained to her that they were confident she could do this task as she was the one who carried Pedro's <a href="/wiki/Inherited_Will" title="Inherited Will">will</a> in her heart and was therefore most qualified.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> He later joined his fellow Scabbards alongside Yamato and Momonosuke when the latter took his place as the new Shogun of Wano.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Final_Saga">Final Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="Oni_Child_Yamato.27s_Golden_Harvest_Surrogate_Pilgrimage"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Oni_Child_Yamato's_Golden_Harvest_Surrogate_Pilgrimage">Oni Child Yamato's Golden Harvest Surrogate Pilgrimage</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As Yamato travel his last time in Wano, he payed respect to Nekomamushi with a hug.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Major_Battles">Major Battles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Anime_and_Manga_Differences">Anime and Manga Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Inuarashi and Nekomamushi getting captured by Orochi's forces after Oden's death was first shown in <a href="/wiki/Episode_910" title="Episode 910">Episode 910</a>. However, the manga later revealed that the two minks were captured by a Number.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Merchandise">Merchandise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Video_Games">Video Games</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Playable_Appearances">Playable Appearances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D39&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Thousand_Storm" title="One Piece Thousand Storm">One Piece Thousand Storm</a></i></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Bounty_Rush" title="One Piece Bounty Rush">One Piece Bounty Rush</a></i></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Support_Appearances">Support Appearances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D40&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Great_Pirate_Colosseum" title="One Piece: Great Pirate Colosseum">One Piece: Great Pirate Colosseum</a></i></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D41&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>"Neko Mamushi", although not written in kanji, means "Cat Viper", which the VIZ translation uses. The title of "Master" was added on later.
<ul><li>Brook's voice actor, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ch%C5%8D" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Chō">Chō</a>, made-up a song about "going off to meet the Cat Viper." It impressed Oda enough that he decided to integrate Cat Viper into the manga,<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup> as well as the <a href="/wiki/Let%27s_Go_See_Master_Nekomamushi" title="Let&#39;s Go See Master Nekomamushi">song</a> itself.<sup id="cite_ref-c814b_37-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c814b-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup></li></ul></li>
<li>His design and love of lasagna is similar to the comic strip cat <a href="https://garfield.fandom.com/wiki/Garfield_(character)" class="extiw" title="w:c:garfield:Garfield (character)"><i>Garfield</i></a>.
<ul><li>His use of a smoking pipe may be a reference to a <a href="https://garfield.fandom.com/wiki/File:1978-07-27.gif" class="extiw" title="w:c:garfield:File:1978-07-27.gif">specific Garfield comic strip</a> wherein Garfield takes <a href="https://garfield.fandom.com/wiki/Jon_Arbuckle" class="extiw" title="w:c:garfield:Jon Arbuckle">Jon Arbuckle</a>'s pipe.</li></ul></li>
<li>His design is also similar to the <a href="https://alice.fandom.com/wiki/Cheshire_Cat" class="extiw" title="w:c:alice:Cheshire Cat">Cheshire Cat</a> from <a href="https://alice.fandom.com/wiki/Charles_Dodgson" class="extiw" title="w:c:alice:Charles Dodgson">Lewis Carroll</a>'s <a href="https://alice.fandom.com/wiki/Alice%27s_Adventures_in_Wonderland" class="extiw" title="w:c:alice:Alice&#39;s Adventures in Wonderland"><i>Alice's Adventures in Wonderland</i></a>.</li>
<li>The song he hums while eating in the anime sounds similar to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ludwig_van_Beethoven" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ludwig van Beethoven">Ludwig van Beethoven</a>'s <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Symphony_No._5_(Beethoven)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Symphony No. 5 (Beethoven)">5th Symphony in C minor</a>.</li>
<li>Nekomamushi's height was initially given as 318&#160;cm (10'5") in the <a href="/wiki/Vivre_Card_-_One_Piece_Visual_Dictionary" title="Vivre Card - One Piece Visual Dictionary">Vivre Card databook</a><sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_9-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> before Oda stated his height as 522&#160;cm (17'1") in the <a href="/wiki/SBS_Volume_96" title="SBS Volume 96">SBS Volume 96</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs96_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs96-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Nekomamushi's favorite foods are <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lasagna" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Lasagna">lasagna</a><sup id="cite_ref-c814a_17-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c814a-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_9-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kamaboko" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Kamaboko">kamaboko</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-sbs96_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs96-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> and his least favorite food is anything hot.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_9-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
<ul><li>Fittingly enough, kamaboko is one of the main ingredients in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oden" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Oden">oden</a>, just as Nekomamushi was one of <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden's</a> main retainers.</li>
<li>His dislike of anything hot is likely a reference to the Japanese phrase <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/%E7%8C%AB%E8%88%8C" class="extiw" title="wiktionary:猫舌">"cat tongue" or "cat's tongue"</a></li></ul></li>
<li>Nekomamushi's animal resemblance is a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/European_wildcat" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:European wildcat">wildcat</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_9-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Nekomamushi's hobby is swimming at night.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_9-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Nekomamushi's birthday, November 22, comes from "Good kitty"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">いいにゃんにゃん</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Īnyannyan</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs82_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs82-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="References">References</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNekomamushi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D42&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div style="width:auto; max-height: 230px; overflow:auto; margin-bottom:3px; padding-left:0.5em; border:1px solid #AAAAAA; -moz-border-radius-topleft:0.5em; -webkit-border-top-left-radius:0.5em; border-top-left-radius:0.5em;">
<span style="font-size:x-small"><div class="mw-references-wrap mw-references-columns"><ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-debut-1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">↑ <sup><a href="#cite_ref-debut_1-0">1.0</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-debut_1-1">1.1</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-debut_1-2">1.2</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-debut_1-3">1.3</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-debut_1-4">1.4</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-debut_1-5">1.5</a></sup></span> <span class="reference-text"><i>One Piece</i> Manga&#32;and Anime — <a href="/wiki/Volume_81" title="Volume 81">Vol. 81</a>&#32;<a href="/wiki/Chapter_809" title="Chapter 809">Chapter 809</a>&#32;(p. 15-19)&#32;and <a href="/wiki/Episode_759" title="Episode 759">Episode 759</a>,&#32;Nekomamushi appears for the first time.</span>
</li>
